It is only a 10-minute walk to the former residence of Wang Yangming. The hotel is located on the edge of the Yao River, facing Longquan Mountain across the bank. The hotel has complete facilities and elegant decoration. The underground garage has a second basement floor. The service staff are neatly dressed and polite. The hotel swimming pool is relatively large, the water quality is OK, and there are not many customers. The bathroom in the standard room is also equipped with a bathtub, and the bath products are quite comfortable to use. The air conditioner works well and is very quiet. The bedding is also pretty good, with two pillows and one pillow of each size. The welcome fruit was of poor quality. The taste of the Fulinmen Hong Kong-style tea restaurant on the first floor is good. It is an unexpected surprise to find the long-lost taste of Hong Kong.
